            <span class="sbi-screenreader">How does food affect your mental health? 🧠

@em</span>
            	        <svg style="color: rgba(255,255,255,1)" class="svg-inline--fa fa-play fa-w-14 sbi_playbtn" aria-label="Play" aria-hidden="true" data-fa-processed="" data-prefix="fa" data-icon="play" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512"><path fill="currentColor" d="M424.4 214.7L72.4 6.6C43.8-10.3 0 6.1 0 47.9V464c0 37.5 40.7 60.1 72.4 41.3l352-208c31.4-18.5 31.5-64.1 0-82.6z"></path></svg>            <img src="https://www.emilieeats.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="How does food affect your mental health? 🧠

@emilieeats, an intuitive eating expert and nutritionist, shares the top 3 ways food impacts your mental health 👇

1. ✨Eating enough✨ Consistent energy is key to avoiding blood sugar spikes and crashes. 

If eating enough is hard due to your schedule, stock freezer with delicious and easy food options, such as Tattooed Chef!

2. ✨Eating a variety of foods✨ The gut loves a wide variety of foods, but it especially loves fiber! Many of Tattooed Chef meals contain fibrous foods, like chickpeas, cauliflower, and sweet potatoes.

3. ✨No unnecessary food restrictions✨ Having a stressful relationship with food can negatively impact our mental health. Try making peace with foods you feel guilty eating. When eating becomes more enjoyable &amp; less stressful, our mental health benefits from this. 

@tattooedcheffoods #tattooedchefpartner">

Fairtrade America partners with farmers versus exploits them, plus promotes better working conditions while tackling important issues such as gender inequality, child labor, and climate change. 🌎

            <span class="sbi-screenreader">need a crowd-pleasing dip? Try this vegan buffalo </span>
            	        <svg style="color: rgba(255,255,255,1)" class="svg-inline--fa fa-play fa-w-14 sbi_playbtn" aria-label="Play" aria-hidden="true" data-fa-processed="" data-prefix="fa" data-icon="play" role="presentation" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512"><path fill="currentColor" d="M424.4 214.7L72.4 6.6C43.8-10.3 0 6.1 0 47.9V464c0 37.5 40.7 60.1 72.4 41.3l352-208c31.4-18.5 31.5-64.1 0-82.6z"></path></svg>            <img src="https://www.emilieeats.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="need a crowd-pleasing dip? Try this vegan buffalo chicken dip (!!!) served w/ @CrunchmasterCrackers Multi-Grain Sea Salt Crackers! #ad 🔥🔥🔥⁠⠀
⁠⠀
these crackers are truly SO crunchy &amp; made w/ wholesome ingredients like brown rice, oat fiber, &amp; flax seeds. find them in the cracker aisle at @target &amp; a variety of other grocery stores.⁠⠀
⁠⠀
here’s the recipe:⁠⠀
@CrunchmasterCrackers Multi-Grain Sea Salt Crackers⁠⠀
1 20-oz can jackfruit in brine (drained)⁠⠀
1 c raw cashews, boiled for 10 mins⁠⠀
½ c unsweetened non-dairy milk⁠⠀
½ c buffalo sauce⁠⠀
2 tbsp lemon juice⁠⠀
½ tsp garlic powder⁠⠀
¼ tsp salt⁠⠀
Dash black pepper⁠⠀
⁠⠀
1. For each piece of jackfruit, cut off the harder bit, then shred the rest with your fingers into the bowl. Then, cut up all the harder bits into smaller pieces &amp; add to the bowl.⁠⠀
2. Add cashews &amp; milk to a blender. Blend until smooth.⁠⠀
3. To a baking dish, add cashew cream, jackfruit, buffalo sauce, lemon juice, garlic powder, salt, &amp; pepper. Stir.⁠⠀
4. Bake at 350ºF for 35-40 minutes. Top with green onions &amp; serve with @CrunchmasterCrackers Multi-Grain Sea Salt Crackers!⁠⠀
⁠⠀
#CrunchinBreak">
